<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200"></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cat" class="extiw" title="w:cat">cat</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cat" class="extiw" title="w:cat">Wikipedia </a></span></div>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English" class="extiw" title="w:American English">US</a><span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English" class="extiw" title="w:British English">UK</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">kăt</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/kæt/</span>, <span class="IPA">[kʰæt]</span>, <span class="IPA">[kʰæt̚]</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/cat#Middle_English" title="cat">cat</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/catte#Middle_English" title="catte">catte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/catt#Old_English" title="catt">catt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">male cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/catte#Old_English" title="catte">catte</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">female cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz">*kattuz</a></i>.
</p>
<div class="NavFrame">
<div class="NavHead" style="text-align: left; cursor: pointer;"><span class="NavToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">show ▼</a></span>Further etymology and cognates.</div>
<div class="NavContent derivedterms" style="text-align: left; column-count: 2; display: none;">
<p>The Germanic word is generally thought to be from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/cattus#Latin" title="cattus">cattus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">domestic cat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (c. 350, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rutilius_Taurus_Aemilianus_Palladius" class="extiw" title="w:Rutilius Taurus Aemilianus Palladius">Palladius</a>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/catta#Latin" title="catta">catta</a></i> (c. 75 <span style="font-size:85%;">A.D.</span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Martial" class="extiw" title="w:Martial">Martial</a>),<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> from an <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afroasiatic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Afroasiatic languages">Afroasiatic</a></span> language. This would roughly match how domestic cats themselves spread, as genetic studies suggest they began to spread out of the <a href="/wiki/Near_East" title="Near East">Near East</a> / <a href="/wiki/Fertile_Crescent" title="Fertile Crescent">Fertile Crescent</a> during the Neolithic (being in Cyprus by 9500 years ago,<sup id="cite_ref-ISample_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ISample-2">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-COttoni_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COttoni-3">[3]</a></sup> and Greece and Italy by 2500 years ago<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup>), especially after they became popular in Egypt.<sup id="cite_ref-ISample_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ISample-2">[2]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-COttoni_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COttoni-3">[3]</a></sup> However, every proposed source word has presented problems. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adolphe_Pictet" class="extiw" title="w:Adolphe Pictet">Adolphe Pictet</a><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> and many subsequent sources refer to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barabra" class="extiw" title="w:Barabra">Barabra</a> (Nubian) <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="onw-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kaddîska</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and "Nouba" (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nobiin_language" class="extiw" title="w:Nobiin language">Nobiin</a>) <i class="Latn mention" lang="fia"><a href="/w/index.php?title=kad%C4%ABs&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="kadīs (page does not exist)">kadīs</a></i> as possible sources or cognates,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> but M. Lionel Bender says the Nubian word is a loan from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar"><a href="/wiki/%D9%82%D8%B7%D8%A9#Arabic" title="قطة">قِطَّة</a></i>‎ <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qiṭṭa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-Qitta_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Qitta-7">[7]</a></sup> Jean-Paul Savignac suggests the Latin word is from an Egyptian precursor of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Coptic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Coptic language">Coptic</a></span> <i class="Copt mention" lang="cop"><a href="/wiki/%CF%A3%E2%B2%81%E2%B2%A9#Coptic" title="ϣⲁⲩ">ϣⲁⲩ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cop-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šau</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tomcat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> suffixed with feminine <i class="Latinx mention" lang="egy"><a href="/wiki/-t#Egyptian" title="-t">-t</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> but John Huehnergard says "the source [...] was clearly not Egyptian itself, where no analogous form is attested."<sup id="cite_ref-Qitta_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Qitta-7">[7]</a></sup>
</p><p>It may be a <a href="/wiki/Wanderwort" title="Wanderwort">Wanderwort</a><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> Kroonen says the word must have existed in Germanic from a very early date, as it shows morphological alternations, and suggests that it might have been borrowed from Uralic, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_Sami" class="extiw" title="w:Northern Sami">Northern Sami</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="se"><a href="/w/index.php?title=ga%C4%91fe&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="gađfe (page does not exist)">gađfe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">female stoat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hungarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hungarian language">Hungarian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hu"><a href="/wiki/h%C3%B6lgy#Hungarian" title="hölgy">hölgy</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stoat; lady, bride</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Uralic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Uralic language">Proto-Uralic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="urj-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Uralic/k%C3%A4%C4%8Fw%C3%A4" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Uralic/käďwä">*käďwä</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">female (of a fur animal)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup>
</p><p>Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href="/wiki/%D0%BA%D0%BE%D1%82#Russian" title="кот">кот</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href="/wiki/%D0%BA%D1%96%D1%82#Ukrainian" title="кіт">кіт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kit</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be"><a href="/wiki/%D0%BA%D0%BE%D1%82#Belarusian" title="кот">кот</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl"><a href="/wiki/kot#Polish" title="kot">kot</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kashubian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kashubian language">Kashubian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="csb"><a href="/wiki/k%C3%B2t#Kashubian" title="kòt">kòt</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt"><a href="/wiki/kat%C4%97#Lithuanian" title="katė">katė</a></i>, and more distantly <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Armenian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Armenian language">Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="hy"><a href="/wiki/%D5%AF%D5%A1%D5%BF%D5%B8%D6%82#Armenian" title="կատու">կատու</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hy-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Basque_language" class="extiw" title="w:Basque language">Basque</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="eu"><a href="/wiki/katu#Basque" title="katu">katu</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he"><a href="/wiki/%D7%97%D7%AA%D7%95%D7%9C#Hebrew" title="חתול">חתול</a></i>‎ <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khatúl</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar"><a href="/wiki/%D9%82%D8%B7%D8%A9#Arabic" title="قطة">قِطَّة</a></i>‎ <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qiṭṭa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> alongside dialectal Maghrebi Arabic <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar"><a href="/wiki/%D9%82%D8%B7%D9%88%D8%B3#Arabic" title="قطوس">قَطُّوس</a></i>‎ <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qaṭṭūs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from Berber, probably from Latin).
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catte#English" title="catte">catte</a></span> (<i>obsolete</i>)</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cats#English" title="cats">cats</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An animal of the family <a href="/wiki/Felidae" title="Felidae">Felidae</a>:
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b>,  Karl Kruszelnicki,  <cite>Brain Food</cite>, <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/1466828129" title="Special:BookSources/1466828129">→ISBN</a></small>, page 53:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Mammals need two genes to make the taste receptor for sugar. Studies in various <b>cats</b> (tigers, cheetahs and domestic cats) showed that one of these genes has mutated and no longer works.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/felid#English" title="felid">felid</a></span></span></dd></dl>
<ol><li>A domesticated <a href="/wiki/species" title="species">species</a> (<i><a href="/wiki/Felis_catus" title="Felis catus">Felis catus</a></i>) or <a href="/wiki/subspecies" title="subspecies">subspecies</a> (<i><a href="/wiki/Felis_silvestris_catus" title="Felis silvestris catus">Felis silvestris catus</a></i>) of <a href="/wiki/feline" title="feline">feline</a> animal, commonly kept as a house <a href="/wiki/pet" title="pet">pet</a>. <span class="defdate">[from 8<sup>th</sup>c.]</span>
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1892</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_Besant" class="extiw" title="w:Walter Besant">Walter Besant</a>,  chapter II, in  <cite>The Ivory Gate: A Novel</cite>, New York, N.Y.: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harper_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Harper (publisher)">Harper &amp; Brothers</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&nbsp;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Franklin Square">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/16832619">16832619</a></small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>At twilight in the summer there is never anybody to fear—man, woman, or <b>cat</b>—in the chambers and at that hour the mice come out. They do not eat parchment or foolscap or red tape, but they eat the luncheon crumbs.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/puss#English" title="puss">puss</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pussy#English" title="pussy">pussy</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/malkin#English" title="malkin">malkin</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/kitty#English" title="kitty">kitty</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pussy-cat#English" title="pussy-cat">pussy-cat</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/grimalkin#English" title="grimalkin">grimalkin</a></span>; <i>see also</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:cat" title="Thesaurus:cat">Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">cat</span></a></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Any similar animal of the family <a href="/wiki/Felidae" title="Felidae">Felidae</a>, which includes <a href="/wiki/lion" title="lion">lions</a>, <a href="/wiki/tiger" title="tiger">tigers</a>, bobcats, etc.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1977</b>,  Peter Hathaway Capstick,  <cite>Death in the Long Grass: A Big Game Hunter's Adventures in the African Bush</cite>, St. Martin's Press, page 44:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I grabbed it and ran over to the lion from behind, the <b>cat</b> still chewing thoughtfully on Silent's arm.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1985</b> January, George Laycock, "Our American Lion", in Boy Scouts of America, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boys%27_Life" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Boys' Life">Boys' Life</a></i>, 28.
<dl><dd>If you should someday round a corner on the hiking trail and come face to face with a mountain lion, you would probably never forget the mighty <b>cat</b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  Dale Mayer,  <cite>Rare Find. A Psychic Visions Novel</cite>, Valley Publishing:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">She felt privileged to be here, living the experience inside the majestic <b>cat</b> [i.e. a tiger]; privileged to be part of their bond, even for only a few hours.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol></li>
<li>A person:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/offensive" title="offensive">offensive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A spiteful or angry <a href="/wiki/woman" title="woman">woman</a>. <span class="defdate">[from early 13<sup>th</sup>c.]</span>
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1835</b> September, anonymous, "The Pigs", in <i>The New-England Magazine</i>, Vol. 9, 156.
<dl><dd>But, ere one rapid moon its tale has told, / He finds his prize — a <b>cat</b> — a slut — a scold.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bitch#English" title="bitch">bitch</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>An enthusiast or player of <a href="/wiki/jazz" title="jazz">jazz</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nick_Cave_and_the_Bad_Seeds" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nick Cave and the Bad Seeds">Nick Cave and the Bad Seeds</a> (lyrics and music),  “Hold on to Yourself”:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I turn on the radio / There's some <b>cat</b> on the saxophone / Laying down a litany of excuses</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person (usually male).
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1972</b>,  “Starman”, in  <cite>The Rise and Fall of Ziggy Stardust and the Spiders from Mars</cite>, performed by David Bowie:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Didn't know what time it was the lights were low / I leaned back on my radio / Some <b>cat</b> was layin' down some rock'n'roll 'lotta soul, he said</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1973</b> December, "Books Noted", discussing <i>A Dialogue</i> (by James Baldwin and Nikki Giovanni), in <i>Black World</i>, Johnson Publishing Company, 77.
<dl><dd>BALDWIN: That's what we were talking about before. And by the way, you did not have to tell me that you think your father is a groovy <b>cat</b>; I knew that.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1998</b>,  “Fiend”, in  <cite>Respect</cite>, performed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shaquille_O%27Neal" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shaquille O'Neal">Shaquille O'Neal</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">What fags are true I know what Mack's might do<br>I'm quite familiar with <b>cats</b> like you<br>Provoke to get me give me a good reason to smoke me<br>Try to break me but never wrote me)</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2006</b>,  Masta Ace (lyrics),  “Sick of it all”, in  <cite>Pariah</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I am sick of rappers claiming they hot when they really not<br>I am sick of rappers bragging about shit they ain’t really got<br>These <b>cats</b> stay rapping about cars they don’t own<br>I am sick of rappers bragging about models they don’t bone.[…]<br>And I am sick of all these <b>cats</b> with no talent<br>That never lived in the hood but yet their lyrics be so violent.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bloke#English" title="bloke">bloke</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/chap#English" title="chap">chap</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cove#English" title="cove">cove</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/dude#English" title="dude">dude</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/fellow#English" title="fellow">fellow</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/fella#English" title="fella">fella</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/guy#English" title="guy">guy</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/prostitute" title="prostitute">prostitute</a>. <span class="defdate">[from at least early 15<sup>th</sup>c.]</span>
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1999</b>,  Carl P. Willie said there was a <b>cat</b> in love with you. That isn't true, is it?" "Yes. It's true," Hudson corrects her, letting her think that by "cat" he means prostitute.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/nautical" title="nautical">nautical</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A strong tackle used to hoist an anchor to the <a href="/wiki/cathead" title="cathead">cathead</a> of a ship.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  Olof A. Eriksen,  <cite>Constitution - All Sails Up and Flying</cite>, Outskirts Press, page 134:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Overhaul down &amp; hook the <b>cat</b>, haul taut. Walk away the <b>cat</b>. When up, pass the <b>cat</b> head stopper. Hook the fish in &amp; fish the anchor.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="/wiki/nautical" title="nautical">nautical</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Short form of</span> <a href="/wiki/cat-o%27-nine-tails" title="cat-o'-nine-tails">cat-o'-nine-tails</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1839</b>,  <cite>Documents of the Assembly of the State of New York</cite>, testimony by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_L._Pinckney" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry L. Pinckney">Henry L. Pinckney</a> (Assembly No. 335), page 44:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>he whipped a black man for disobedience of his orders fifty lashes; and again whipped him with a <b>cat</b>, which he wound with wire, about the same number of stripes;<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>he used this <b>cat</b> on one other man, and then destroyed the <b>cat</b> wound with wire.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sturdy merchant sailing vessel <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">now only in "<a href="/wiki/catboat" title="catboat">catboat</a>"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The game of "<a href="/w/index.php?title=trap_and_ball&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="trap and ball (page does not exist)">trap and ball</a>" (also called "cat and dog").
<ol><li>The trap of the game of "trap and ball".</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The pointed piece of wood that is struck in the game of <a href="/wiki/tipcat" title="tipcat">tipcat</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#vulgar" title="Appendix:Glossary">vulgar</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/African-American_Vernacular_English" class="extiw" title="w:African-American Vernacular English">African-American Vernacular</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/vagina" title="vagina">vagina</a>, a <a href="/wiki/vulva" title="vulva">vulva</a>; the female external genitalia.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1969</b>,  Iceberg Slim,  <cite>Pimp: The Story of My Life</cite>, Holloway House Publishing:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"What the hell, so this broad's got a prematurely-gray <b>cat</b>."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  Carolyn Chambers Sanders,  <cite>Sins &amp; Secrets</cite>, Hachette Digital:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">As she came up, she tried to put her <b>cat</b> in his face for some licking.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  Franklin White,  <cite>Money for Good</cite>, Simon and Schuster, page 64:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I had a notion to walk over to her, rip her apron off, sling her housecoat open and put my finger inside her <b>cat</b> to see if she was wet or freshly fucked because the dream I had earlier was beginning to really annoy me.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/double" title="double">double</a> <a href="/wiki/tripod" title="tripod">tripod</a> (for holding a <a href="/wiki/plate" title="plate">plate</a>, etc.) with six feet, of which three rest on the ground, in whatever position it is placed.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#historical" title="Appendix:Glossary">historical</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/wheel" title="wheel">wheeled</a> <a href="/wiki/shelter" title="shelter">shelter</a>, used in the <a href="/wiki/Middle_Ages" title="Middle Ages">Middle Ages</a> as a <a href="/wiki/siege" title="siege">siege</a> weapon to allow <a href="/wiki/assailant" title="assailant">assailants</a> to approach enemy <a href="/wiki/defence" title="defence">defences</a>.

<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2000</b>,  Stephen O'Shea,  <cite>The Perfect Heresy</cite>, Profile Books, page 97:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">From behind the narrow slits in the walls of Castellar, crossbowmen and archers took aim at the juddering <b>cat</b> as it came closer.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<dl><dd><i>The terms below need to be checked and allocated to the definitions (senses) of the headword above. Each term should appear in the sense for which it is appropriate. <ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">any member of the <a href="/wiki/suborder" title="suborder">suborder</a> (sometimes <a href="/wiki/superfamily" title="superfamily">superfamily</a>) <a href="/wiki/Feliformia" title="Feliformia">Feliformia</a> or <a href="/wiki/Feloidea" title="Feloidea">Feloidea</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/feliform#English" title="feliform">feliform</a></span> ("<a href="/wiki/cat-like" title="cat-like">cat-like</a>" <a href="/wiki/carnivoran" title="carnivoran">carnivoran</a>), <a href="/wiki/feloid" title="feloid">feloid</a> (compare <a href="/wiki/Caniformia" title="Caniformia">Caniformia</a>, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Canoidea" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Canoidea">Canoidea</a></span>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">any member of the <a href="/wiki/subfamily" title="subfamily">subfamily</a> <a href="/wiki/Felinae" title="Felinae">Felinae</a>, genera <i><a href="/wiki/Puma" title="Puma">Puma</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Acinonyx" title="Acinonyx">Acinonyx</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Lynx" title="Lynx">Lynx</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Leopardus" title="Leopardus">Leopardus</a></i>, and <i><a href="/wiki/Felis" title="Felis">Felis</a></i>)</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/w/index.php?title=feline_cat&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="feline cat (page does not exist)">feline cat</a></span>, a <a href="/wiki/feline" title="feline">feline</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">any member of the subfamily <a href="/wiki/Pantherinae" title="Pantherinae">Pantherinae</a>, genera <i><a href="/wiki/Panthera" title="Panthera">Panthera</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uncia" title="Uncia">Uncia</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Neofelis" title="Neofelis">Neofelis</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/w/index.php?title=pantherine_cat&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="pantherine cat (page does not exist)">pantherine cat</a></span>, a <a href="/wiki/pantherine" title="pantherine">pantherine</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">technically, all members of the genus <i>Panthera</i></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/panther#English" title="panther">panther</a></span> (i.e. <a href="/wiki/tiger" title="tiger">tiger</a>, <a href="/wiki/lion" title="lion">lion</a>, <a href="/wiki/jaguar" title="jaguar">jaguar</a>, <a href="/wiki/leopard" title="leopard">leopard</a>), <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">narrow sense</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/panther" title="panther">panther</a> (i.e. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/black_panther" class="extiw" title="w:black panther">black panther</a>)</li>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Translations">Translations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Translations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>See <a href="/wiki/cat/translations#Noun" title="cat/translations">cat/translations §&nbsp;Noun</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cats#English" title="cats">cats</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catting#English" title="catting">catting</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catted#English" title="catted">catted</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/nautical" title="nautical">nautical</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/hoist" title="hoist">hoist</a> (the <a href="/wiki/anchor" title="anchor">anchor</a>) by its <a href="/wiki/ring" title="ring">ring</a> so that it hangs at the <a href="/wiki/cathead" title="cathead">cathead</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1922</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Lynde" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Francis Lynde">Francis Lynde</a>, <i>Pirates' Hope</i>, Charles Scribner's Sons, New York, page 226:
<dl><dd>The anchors were <b>catted</b> at the bows of the yacht …</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/nautical" title="nautical">nautical</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To flog with a <a href="/wiki/cat-o%27-nine-tails" title="cat-o'-nine-tails">cat-o'-nine-tails</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/vomit" title="vomit">vomit</a>.</li>
<li>To go <a href="/wiki/wander" title="wander">wandering</a> at <a href="/wiki/night" title="night">night</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1998</b>,  Mary Spencer,  <cite>Lady's Wager</cite>, page 324:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">"He doesn't realize that I know," Lord Callan said, "but it's been pretty obvious that most of his <b>catting</b> about London's darker alleys has been a search for his origins.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2010</b>,  Claude Brown,  <cite>Manchild in the Promised Land</cite>, page 18:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">This was going to be my first try at <b>catting</b> out. I went looking for somebody to <b>cat</b> with me.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b>,  Valerie Hansen,  <cite>Wages of Sin</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">My own dear wife could have tended to his needs if she hadn't been out <b>catting</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To <a href="/wiki/gossip" title="gossip">gossip</a> in a <a href="/wiki/catty" title="catty">catty</a> manner.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1932</b>,  Hugh Brooke,  <cite>Man Made Angry</cite>, page 134:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Men from young to middleaged, with matt faces, vivacious and brightly dressed, <b>catted</b> together in gay groups.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1996</b>,  Alistair Boyle,  <cite>The Unlucky Seven</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">They smiled, touched, rolled their eyes and raised their eyebrows, as they relived the audition and <b>catted</b> about some of their competition.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2016</b>,  Melanie Benjamin,  <cite>The Swans of Fifth Avenue</cite>, page 293:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In the story, Lady Ina gossiped and <b>catted</b> about a parade of the rich and famous—Jackie Kennedy looking like an exaggerated version of herself, Princess Margaret so boring she made people fall asleep, Gloria Vanderbilt so ditzy she didn't recognize her first husband.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cats#English" title="cats">cats</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Abbreviation of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catamaran#English" title="catamaran">catamaran</a></i></span></span>.</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Etymology 3">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Abbreviation of <i><a href="/wiki/catenate" title="catenate">catenate</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cats#English" title="cats">cats</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing#Noun" title="computing">computing</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A program and command in <a href="/wiki/Unix" title="Unix">Unix</a> that reads one or more files and directs their content to the standard output.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cats#English" title="cats">cats</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catting#English" title="catting">catting</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catted#English" title="catted">catted</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing#Noun" title="computing">computing</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/apply" title="apply">apply</a> the <b>cat</b> <a href="/wiki/command" title="command">command</a> to (one or more files).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing#Noun" title="computing">computing</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/dump" title="dump">dump</a> large amounts of data on (an unprepared target) usually with no intention of browsing it carefully.</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Etymology 4">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Possibly a shortened form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catastrophic#English" title="catastrophic">catastrophic</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i>not <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparable" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparable</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ireland" class="extiw" title="w:Ireland">Ireland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/terrible" title="terrible">Terrible</a>, <a href="/wiki/disastrous" title="disastrous">disastrous</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The weather was <b>cat</b>, so they returned home early.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>This usage is common in speech but rarely appears in writing.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology 5</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Etymology 5">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Shortened from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/methcathinone#English" title="methcathinone">methcathinone</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">A street name of the drug <a href="/wiki/methcathinone#English" title="methcathinone">methcathinone</a>.</span></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology 6</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Etymology 6">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Abbreviation of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/catfish#English" title="catfish">catfish</a></i></span></span>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Willa_Cather" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Willa Cather">Willa Cather</a>,  chapter 2, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/O_Pioneers!" class="extiw" title="s:O Pioneers!">O Pioneers!</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">She missed the fish diet of her own country, and twice every summer she sent the boys to the river, twenty miles to the southward, to fish for channel <b>cat</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1916</b>, M. Shults, "Fishing for Yellow Cat in the Brazos", in <i>Field and Stream</i>, vol. 21, 478.
<dl><dd>Fishing for <b>cat</b> is probably, up to a certain stage, the least exciting of all similar sports.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_9">Etymology 9</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Etymology 9">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Abbreviation of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/caterpillar#English" title="caterpillar">caterpillar</a></i></span></span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">cat</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cats#English" title="cats">cats</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of a variety of earth-moving <a href="/wiki/machine" title="machine">machines</a>. (from their manufacturer <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caterpillar_Inc." class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Caterpillar Inc.">Caterpillar Inc.</a>)</li>
<li>A <a href="/w/index.php?title=caterpillar_drive&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="caterpillar drive (page does not exist)">caterpillar drive</a> vehicle (a ground vehicle which uses <a href="/wiki/caterpillar_track" title="caterpillar track">caterpillar tracks</a>), especially tractors, trucks, minibuses, and snow groomers.</li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Indonesian">Indonesian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Indonesian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a href="/wiki/cat#Malay" title="cat">cat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Min">Min Nan</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="nan"><a href="/wiki/%E6%BC%86#Min_Nan" title="漆">漆</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="nan-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">chhat</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Chinese">Middle Chinese</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="ltc"><a href="/wiki/%E6%BC%86#Middle_Chinese" title="漆">漆</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ltc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tsit</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_10">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Malay">Malay</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Malay">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:GreenPaintBucketRome.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/GreenPaintBucketRome.jpg/200px-GreenPaintBucketRome.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="267" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/GreenPaintBucketRome.jpg/300px-GreenPaintBucketRome.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/GreenPaintBucketRome.jpg/400px-GreenPaintBucketRome.jpg 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="800"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:GreenPaintBucketRome.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>cat</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_11">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Min" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Min">Min Nan</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="nan"><a href="/wiki/%E6%BC%86#Min_Nan" title="漆">漆</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="nan-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">chhat</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Chinese">Middle Chinese</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="ltc"><a href="/wiki/%E6%BC%86#Middle_Chinese" title="漆">漆</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ltc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tsit</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_4">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_11">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="ms">cat</strong> (<i>Jawi spelling</i> <b class="ms-Arab" lang="ms"><a href="/wiki/%DA%86%D8%AA#Malay" title="چت">چت</a></b>‎, <i>informal 1st possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="ms">cat<a href="/wiki/-ku#Malay" title="-ku">ku</a></b>, <i>impolite 2nd possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="ms">cat<a href="/wiki/-mu#Malay" title="-mu">mu</a></b>, <i>3rd possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="ms">cat<a href="/wiki/-nya#Malay" title="-nya">nya</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/paint" title="paint">paint</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">substance</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Affixed_terms_2">Affixed terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Affixed terms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/bercat" title="bercat">bercat</a></li>
<li>mengecat <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Active_voice" class="extiw" title="w:Active voice">active</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>: to paint
<ul><li>dicat <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Passive_voice" class="extiw" title="w:Passive voice">passive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>: to be painted</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="ms"><a href="/wiki/catan#Malay" title="catan">catan</a></span>: <a href="/wiki/painting" title="painting">painting</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an artwork in the form of a painted picture</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=pengecatan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="pengecatan (page does not exist)">pengecatan</a>: the <a href="/wiki/action" title="action">action</a> of applying paint to something (e.g. a surface, etc.)</li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=pengecat&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="pengecat (page does not exist)">pengecat</a>: <a href="/wiki/painter" title="painter">painter</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a person whose job is paining buildings</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_12">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/catt#Old_English" title="catt">catt</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/catte#Old_English" title="catte">catte</a></i>; this is in turn from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/kattuz">*kattuz</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Norman">Norman</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Norman">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_13">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norman" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norman">Old Northern French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/cat#Old_French" title="cat">cat</a></i> (variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/chat#Old_French" title="chat">chat</a></i>) from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/cattus#Latin" title="cattus">cattus</a></i>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_13">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nrf">cat</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nrf p-form-of" lang="nrf"><a href="/wiki/cats#Norman" title="cats">cats</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nrf"><a href="/wiki/catte#Norman" title="catte">catte</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cat#English" title="cat">cat</a></span>
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary">c.</a></i> <b>1830</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_M%C3%A9tivier" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:George Métivier">George Métivier</a>, ‘Lamentations de Damaris’:
<dl><dd>Où'est donc qu'j'iron, mé et mes puches / Ma <b>catte</b>, et l'reste de l'écu?</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2006</b>, Peggy Collenette, ‘D'la gâche de Guernési’, <i>P'tites Lures Guernésiaises</i>, Cromwell Press 2006, page 20:
<dl><dd>Ils d'visirent pour enne haeure, mais la Louise était pas chagrinaïe au tour sa pâte, pasqué a savait que le <b>cat</b> était à gardaïr la pâte caoude. (<i>They talked for an hour, but Louise was not worried about her dough, because she knew that the <b>cat</b> was keeping the dough warm.</i>)</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jersey" class="extiw" title="w:Jersey">Jersey</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/common_dab" class="extiw" title="w:common dab">common dab</a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Limanda_limanda" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Limanda limanda"><i>Limanda limanda</i></a></span>)</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nrf"><a href="/wiki/catchi%C3%A9the#Norman" title="catchiéthe">catchiéthe</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cat-flap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Old_French">Old French</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Old French">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_14">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fro">cat</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>oblique plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/caz#Old_French" title="caz">caz</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=catz&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="catz (page does not exist)">catz</a></b>, <i>nominative singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/caz#Old_French" title="caz">caz</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=catz&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="catz (page does not exist)">catz</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><strong class="selflink">cat</strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Picardy" class="extiw" title="w:Picardy">Picardy</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/chat#Old_French" title="chat">chat</a></i></span></span></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Romanian">Romanian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Romanian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_14">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr"><a href="/wiki/kat#Turkish" title="kat">kat</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_7">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Romanian_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Romanian pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/kat/</span></li>
<li>Rhymes: <a href="/wiki/Rhymes:Romanian/at" title="Rhymes:Romanian/at"><span class="IPA">-at</span></a></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_15">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="ro">cat</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-ro p-form-of" lang="ro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=caturi&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="caturi (page does not exist)">caturi</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dated" title="Appendix:Glossary">dated</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/floor" title="floor">floor</a> (<a href="/wiki/storey" title="storey">storey</a>)
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1892</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbu_%C8%98tef%C4%83nescu_Delavrancea" class="extiw" title="w:Barbu Ștefănescu Delavrancea">Barbu Ștefănescu Delavrancea</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ro:Domnul_Vucea" class="extiw" title="s:ro:Domnul Vucea">Mr. Vucea</a></i>:
<dl><dd>Mi-aduc bine aminte că unul sărea de la al cincilea <b>cat</b>, și c-o mână își ținea pălăria. Grozav îi era de pălărie!
<dl><dd>I remember well that one was jumping from the fifth <b>floor</b>, and was holding his hat with one hand. That proud was he of the hat!</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Scottish_Gaelic">Scottish Gaelic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: Scottish Gaelic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg/170px-Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="227" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg/255px-Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg/340px-Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg 2x" data-file-width="950" data-file-height="1267"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Stray_calico_cat_near_Sagami_River-01.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Cat.</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_15">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=75" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/catt#Old_Irish" title="catt">catt</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/cattus#Latin" title="cattus">cattus</a></i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Irish language">Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga"><a href="/wiki/cat#Irish" title="cat">cat</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Manx_language" class="extiw" title="w:Manx language">Manx</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gv"><a href="/wiki/kayt#Manx" title="kayt">kayt</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_8">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=76" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Scottish_Gaelic_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Scottish Gaelic pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/kʰaʰt̪/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_16">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=cat&amp;action=edit&amp;section=77" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="gd">cat</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>genitive singular</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-gd gen|s-form-of" lang="gd"><a href="/wiki/cait#Scottish_Gaelic" title="cait">cait</a></b>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-gd p-form-of" lang="gd"><a href="/wiki/cait#Scottish_Gaelic" title="cait">cait</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="#English">cat</a> <i>(<a href="/wiki/Felis_catus" title="Felis catus">Felis catus</a>)</i></li></ol>
